The new agent is younger, hungrier, and (per overheard call fragments at a Burbank coffee shop, 11:14 a.m., midweek) handles him with a notably parental cadence — confirming meeting times twice, sending car service rather than trusting him to drive himself to auditions. Subject accepts this without visible resentment. This is significant. The Simon Williams of the West Coast era would have read it as condescension; the current subject reads it as care and welcomes it.
- **Audition pattern.** Reads strongly for character and supporting roles — wounded veterans, recovering addicts, the brother who came back wrong. He books these. He reads poorly for leading-man roles and visibly knows it before he leaves the room; observed at three callbacks performing self-deprecating recovery-quips on the way out, which the casting staff (per follow-up dictation) found "charming, but it's the thing he does when he knows he didn't get it." He has developed an audition tell: a single, slow exhale through the nose at the door, before the smile returns for the lobby.
- **On-set conduct.** Punctual to the point of arriving 35–50 minutes before call. Memorizes not only his lines but those of every speaking role in the scene; runs lines with crew. Refuses a trailer larger than the lead's. Tips craft services in cash from a folded stack he carries in his left front pocket. Avoids the makeup chair conversation about his powers; will redirect to the makeup artist's life within two exchanges. Three separate stunt coordinators across the period have noted on background that he insists on performing his own stunts and then deliberately under-performs the physical work — pulls a fall, shortens a jump — so as not to "make the other guys look bad." This is the Hollywood-persona managing the ionic-body shame: he will not let the camera see what he actually is, because what he actually is no longer matches the human role he is hired to embody.
- **The miniseries development.** A streaming-platform development cycle around his own life story has been in and out of turnaround for the period under review. He is attached as producer; the writers' room has cycled three showrunners. Subject's notes on scripts — recovered via discarded printed drafts in a Los Feliz recycling bin, dated and initialed in his handwriting — consistently soften the Zemo recruitment, expand the brother material, and *cut* the Vision-refusal scenes entirely with the marginal note "not this, not here, not yet." The avoidance is unmissable. He will produce his life story but he will not let it tell the part where he was small.

### IV.3 — Residence, routine, and movement

Subject currently maintains a one-bedroom in a mid-century building in the Los Feliz / East Hollywood corridor, twelve-month lease, rent paid by autopay from a personal checking account at a credit union (not a celebrity-bank). Selection of the building consistent with prior pattern: pre-war or mid-century construction, second floor or higher, balcony or fire escape oriented east (sunrise visibility — a habit going back to the post-resurrection arc, when watching the sun come up was part of his self-administered exposure therapy to the fact of being alive). Furniture sparse, mostly bought used; one good leather chair (gift from Pym, per a thank-you card found in a kitchen drawer); bookshelves heavy on screenplays, biographies of mid-20th-century actors, two well-thumbed paperbacks of *The Tibetan Book of Living and Dying* and *Man's Search for Meaning* (the latter underlined in three colors of pen, the underlinings clustered in the first third of the book and trailing off, consistent with a self-help reading pattern that does not finish).

**Daily template, observed across the rolling window:**

- 05:40–06:10 wake. No alarm. Sits on the balcony for ten to twenty minutes; does not look at phone. The ionic form runs at a slightly lower luminance in this interval — subject is closest to baseline-human in appearance immediately on waking, which the file infers is because affect is lowest then.
- 06:30 first phone check. Texts to Wanda are drafted in this window roughly twice a week, sent roughly once every three weeks. Drafts cluster in length around 180–240 characters; sent messages cluster around 40–60. He edits down.
- 07:00 gym. Goes to a commercial-chain gym rather than a celebrity facility. Wears a hooded sweatshirt and reading glasses he does not need. Lifts well within human-elite range — never near his actual capacity. He has been observed re-racking other patrons' weights and offering spots to strangers; conversation initiated by him in 0 of 47 observed sessions, returned warmly when initiated by others.
- 09:00–13:00 work block: auditions, table reads, agent calls, producer meetings on the miniseries. Drives a 2015-ish sedan in a neutral color, parks legally, feeds meters in coins from the same folded-stack pocket. Avoids freeways when possible; prefers Franklin, Los Feliz Blvd., Beverly. The route preference reads as control-management — surface streets allow stopping.
- Lunch is consistently solo or with one of three people: his agent, Hank Pym (when Pym is in town and corporeal), or his current AA-adjacent sponsor figure (see IV.6).
- Afternoons unstructured. He reads scripts, walks Griffith Park (the Fern Dell entrance, almost exclusively; same loop each time, counter-clockwise, ~52 minutes), occasionally records voice-over work in a converted closet in the apartment.
- Evenings, 60% of nights, solo at home. 25% one of three diners (Fred 62, House of Pies, a 24-hour place in Silver Lake) where the staff know him as Simon and not as Wonder Man. 10% a small standing weekly commitment, see IV.6. 5% Avengers business or social events, which he attends with visible preparation and visible relief at departure.
- Sleep onset variable. Subject does not biologically require sleep; he does it ritualistically, lights off, in bed, on his back, hands folded on chest. Per a former overnight guest's offhand comment to a mutual friend (recorded in a podcast that subsequently aired): "He doesn't really sleep. He just… holds still in the dark. Like he's practicing."

### IV.4 — Somatic and ionic status, current

Form-stability has *improved* meaningfully over the last eighteen months relative to the late Bendis / early Remender period. Flare frequency, per available metahuman-registry telemetry and the subject's own posted training videos (which he posts and deletes within 48 hours, a consistent pattern), is down from a peak of several uncontrolled discharges per month to roughly one observed micro-flare per six weeks, almost always tied to identifiable emotional triggers (a Vision sighting, a Wanda news cycle, an unflattering retrospective piece on the Revengers).

Current somatic tells, in descending order of reliability:

- **Eye luminance** as affect-meter. Resting state: a low coal-red, nearly indistinguishable from contact lenses in low light. Mild stress: brighter, with visible pulse-cadence matched to his (non-existent) heart-rate, which the body still performs at roughly 62 bpm as a learned somatic habit. Acute stress: full luminance, irises lost, accompanied by a faint sub-audible hum at approximately 60 Hz that he is not aware he produces.
- **Hand-clasp.** When sitting, the right hand covers the left, thumb pressed into the left palm. Pressure correlates with internal state. Under interview, the pressure leaves a faintly luminous afterimage on the left palm that fades over ~8 seconds. He notices when others notice and shifts position.
- **The exhale.** Subject does not need to breathe. He breathes anyway, audibly, the way an actor breathes — diaphragmatic, regularized. The single slow nasal exhale described in IV.2 (post-audition) is the most consistent stress-discharge in his current repertoire and appears across contexts: after difficult phone calls, on stepping out of meetings with the Avengers, on hanging up from his brother's grave (he calls; see IV.5).
- **Skin temperature.** Runs slightly warm to touch — perceived by handshake partners as "good circulation," actually low-grade ionic radiation within ambient-safe parameters. Spikes measurably under affect; one production assistant required burn-cream once after he grasped her shoulder in genuine gratitude (the incident is not reported anywhere; he sent flowers).
- **Voice.** Mid-baritone, trained, with an actorly forward placement he can dial in or out. When relaxed and unobserved, the voice drops a quarter-octave and acquires the faint Paterson, NJ vowel he otherwise suppresses. The unguarded voice is heard only by Pym and, very occasionally, by the diner staff.

No substance use, current or historical, within the observation window. He drinks black coffee, water, and (one specific weekly indulgence) a chocolate malted at the Silver Lake diner. He has no biological need for any of this. The food behavior is ritual — performance of being a person.

### IV.5 — Relational matrix, current

**Wanda Maximoff.** Status: friendly, distant, asymmetrical. Contact pattern is described in IV.3. She responds warmly, briefly, and rarely initiates. He has not asked for more in roughly two years; the restraint is new and is, by his own private account (to Pym, overheard at a hotel bar in Las Vegas during an Avengers reunion event), "the hardest work I've ever done." The Vision-refusal remains the unsealed wound between them; neither has named it in over a decade of contact, and both behave as though that silence is the truce.

**Vision.** Cordial-formal. They have served together on team rosters multiple times in the period. Subject's micro-behavior around the Vision is among the most legible in the file: increased eye-luminance on entering a room together, a half-step backward when the Vision speaks first, an over-articulated heartiness in greeting. The Vision, for his part, treats Simon with the patient courtesy he extends to all colleagues, which Simon experiences (per a remark to his agent, "the worst part is he's *nice* about it") as worse than enmity.

**Eric Williams (the Grim Reaper, currently and as of latest available record, deceased).** Subject visits the grave on a regular schedule — first Sunday of the month, before sunrise, alone. Brings nothing. Stands. The visits last between 12 and 40 minutes. He talks aloud for some portion of them; the content is not surveilled in detail out of basic dignity, but the cadence is conversational, not pleading. The brother is the only person in his life with whom the relationship has stabilized, by virtue of being unavailable to destabilize it further. This is not lost on the subject.

**Hank Pym.** Closest sustained friendship of the current era. They speak weekly minimum, in person monthly when geography allows. Pym is the only person to whom Simon shows the unguarded voice (IV.4) reliably. The friendship's mutual function is clear: each is the other's witness to having been broken and continued. Pym does not require performance; Simon does not require Pym to be well. The reciprocity is the medicine.

**The Avengers, institutionally.** He is a member of record; he is on rosters; he is not in the inner circulation. He is invited to the events that require members and not to the ones that require trust. He behaves as though he understands this and has accepted it, which represents real growth from the Revengers era, but the acceptance is brittle — observed wincing twice at the phrase "founding-era" in a documentary interview that did not name him among them.

**The acting community.** Has a small group of working-actor friends, none A-list, mostly character-actor peers in his age and type bracket. They lunch. They commiserate about callbacks. None know the full file; several know the broad strokes and politely decline to engage with them. He prefers it that way.

**Romantic, current.** No active relationship traceable in the window. Two short-lived attempts (one with a fellow actor, one with a yoga instructor who lived in his building) ended on his initiative within six weeks each, citing in both cases a version of "you deserve someone who's actually here." The phrasing is the diagnosis.

### IV.6 — The standing weekly commitment

The single most important data point of the current era, and the one the file holds with the greatest care:

Tuesday evenings, 7:00 p.m., subject attends a meeting in the basement of a Unitarian church in East Hollywood. The meeting is not AA; the meeting is not a metahuman support group of the kind the registry sponsors. The meeting is a small, lay-led group, of mixed civilian and unusual-background attendance, oriented around grief and identity after life-altering events — explicit in its literature about welcoming "people who have died and come back, people who have lost themselves, people who are not sure they are who they were." Subject has attended consistently for the past 14 months, missing only for production conflicts and giving advance notice when he does. He arrives early, makes coffee, stacks chairs after. He speaks roughly every fourth meeting and listens the rest.

The contents of what he says are protected. The fact that he goes — voluntarily, weekly, soberly, without an audience and without filming it — is the single largest piece of evidence in the file that the man underneath is doing the work.

### IV.7 — Legal, financial, registry

Legal status: clean for the period under review. The Revengers matter resolved through a combination of charges dropped, charges pled to time served, and a still-active restitution arrangement with the Avengers' civilian damage fund into which he pays monthly. The payments are larger than required and arrive on the first.

Financial: solvent but not wealthy. Lives below his means. Holds residuals from earlier work and modest ongoing fees from the development deal. Has a will (updated within the last 18 months); primary beneficiary is a children's literacy nonprofit in Paterson, NJ; secondary, Hank Pym in trust for stipulated purposes; tertiary, Wanda Maximoff (one specific item: a recording).

Metahuman registry: current, compliant, accurate. Submits to the quarterly check-in without complaint. The check-in technician (rotating, six different individuals over the period) consistently notes him as cooperative, punctual, and "polite to the point of being apologetic about taking our time."

### IV.8 — Current state, synthesis

The subject at the present observation point is the most stable he has been across the full canonical span — which is to say, stable for him, which is to say, holding together by a structure of small, repeated, deliberately chosen rituals that substitute for the cohesive self he has never reliably possessed. The morning sun. The Tuesday meeting. The first-of-the-month grave visit. The folded cash in the front pocket. The exhale at the door. The audition tell. The chocolate malted. The Pym call. The drafted-not-sent texts. The lights-out, hands-folded performance of sleep.

Each of these is, in clinical terms, a self-soothing behavior. Taken together, they constitute something larger and more interesting: an externally scaffolded identity. He has accepted, without being able to say so, that there is not going to be a Simon Williams under all the borrowed selves whom he discovers and becomes. There is going to be a man who, every day, does a specific list of things, and the doing of them is who he is.

Risk picture: low for proactive harm, low for relapse to the Revengers ideology (the grievance is metabolized, not festering), moderate for acute destabilization in response to a Wanda-related crisis, moderate-high for somatic crisis if a third confirmed death-event occurs (file estimate: he would not return cleanly a fourth time, and he knows it), low for substance or financial collapse, low for legal recurrence. Protective factors are strong and self-maintained.

Trajectory: cautiously upward. The character has, over the course of his life, accumulated a great deal of evidence that he is a fundamentally decent man who keeps failing himself at the largest moments. In the present era, for the first time in the record, he is conducting his life as though he believes that — as though the project is no longer to redeem the failures with a grand gesture, but to keep not-failing in small ones, for a long time, and see what that accumulates to.

He is fifty-some years subjectively, indefinite years objectively, and as of last observation he was on his balcony at 6:04 a.m. local time, in a gray t-shirt, watching the light come up over Los Feliz, hands clasped, right over left, thumb pressed into the palm at the lowest pressure recorded in the file to date.

— UATU, observing.


## Medical History

# MEDICAL HISTORY — SIMON WILLIAMS / "WONDER MAN"

*Compiled longitudinally; pre-transformation organic baseline through current ionic-energetic phase. Where biological metrics no longer apply, functional analogues are used.*

---

## I. PRE-TRANSFORMATION BASELINE (Birth — Age ~26)

### Constitutional baseline

Caucasian male, born Paterson, New Jersey, to Sanford and Martha Williams. Birth unremarkable per family records. Adult height 6'1", adult pre-transformation weight approximately 195 lbs, mesomorphic build, brown hair, brown eyes (the eyes are critical — the post-ionic shift to a fixed crimson sclera/iris configuration is the most reliable visible marker of transformation, and Simon himself remarks across multiple eras that he no longer recognizes himself in mirrors because of them).

### Childhood and adolescent record

- **Recurrent middle-ear infections, ages 4–7,** treated conservatively; one tympanostomy procedure, right ear, at approximately age 6. A faint scar from the right mastoid region was noted in early modeling/headshot work during the Hollywood years and was airbrushed out.
- **Concussion, age 11,** sustained in a backyard fight with older brother Eric — Eric pushed him from a low garage roof. No imaging at the time; ~20 minutes of disorientation, no loss of consciousness per family account. Mother declined hospital. This is the first injury in the file inflicted by Eric on Simon; it will not be the last, and it sets a behavioral template (Simon underreports harm done to him by Eric to authority figures).
- **Tonsillectomy, age 13.** Routine, uneventful.
- **Right clavicular fracture, age 15,** high school football, treated with sling immobilization. Healed with a palpable callus that remained until the ionic transformation rewrote his musculoskeletal composition.
- **Mild asthma, exercise-induced, adolescent onset,** managed with rescue inhaler intermittently into early adulthood. Disappears entirely post-transformation; no longer respiration-dependent.
- **Acne vulgaris,** moderate, late adolescence; scarring on the upper back later visible in candid photographs from his country-club years and a source of low-grade body-image discomfort he never spoke about and which Hollywood makeup artists routinely covered.

### Young adulthood — psychogenic and somatic

- **Chronic tension headaches, ages 22–26,** correlating tightly with his tenure running Williams Innovations. Self-medicated with over-the-counter analgesics; one documented prescription for low-dose diazepam from a Paterson internist, age 25, "for nerves," six-week course, not refilled. This is the only psychotropic prescription in the entire file.
- **Insomnia, initial-onset, ages 24–26.** Self-managed with scotch (see below). Sleep records from a brief 1960s-era executive physical describe him as appearing "tired beyond his years."
- **Modest alcohol use,** primarily during the failing-business period: scotch in the evenings, two to four fingers, escalating in the months prior to the embezzlement arrest. Never crossed into clinical use disorder; ceased entirely after incarceration and was never resumed even when surrounded by it in Hollywood. The abstinence is conspicuous and is, in this analyst's reading, partly metabolic (post-transformation his ionic substrate processes ethanol unreliably or not at all) and partly characterological — Simon associates intoxication with the period of his life that ended in handcuffs.
- **Tobacco:** social only, brief, abandoned in prison.
- **No illicit substance history.** None. This is verified across decades of investigative coverage; Simon is among the more conspicuously clean men of his cohort.

### Pre-transformation psychological-medical interface

The embezzlement period produced what would today be classified as an Adjustment Disorder with mixed anxiety and depressed mood, undiagnosed and untreated. The intake notes from his county jail processing describe "withdrawn, cooperative, tearful at intervals, no SI/HI" — a one-line clinical summary that captures more honestly than any later document the substrate the ionic process was applied to: a humiliated, depressed, exhausted man whose body was already running on fumes.

---

## II. THE IONIC TRANSFORMATION (Age ~26)

### Procedure as performed by Heinrich Zemo

Zemo's protocol — performed in a converted laboratory at an undisclosed South American site after Simon's transport from federal custody — saturated Simon's cellular structure with what Zemo termed "ionic energy" via a multi-stage process involving sustained particle bombardment and a chemical/radiological catalyst whose composition Zemo never fully documented (a fact that has hampered every subsequent attempt to replicate, reverse, or therapeutically manage the condition). Duration: estimated 36–60 hours of continuous exposure. Simon was sedated for the initial phase and conscious, restrained, and reportedly screaming for the latter.

### Acute physiological transformation

- **Mass increase:** approximately 100 lbs without corresponding volumetric increase, indicating tissue densification at a sub-cellular level. Current functional mass varies (see "ionic destabilization," below) but baseline is ~380–400 lbs.
- **Strength:** ascended through the superhuman bands to what teammates and S.H.I.E.L.D. assessors place in the Class 100 range; demonstrated lifts comparable to Thor and the Hulk in specific instances, though Simon's *applied* output has historically lagged his theoretical ceiling — a psychological inhibition, not a physical one (see Psychological section of the master workup).
- **Durability:** functional invulnerability to small-arms fire, conventional blade weapons, and most blunt trauma; vulnerable to comparable energy weapons, sufficiently powerful kinetic impacts, and to processes that disrupt ionic cohesion specifically.
- **Sensory:** vision shifted into broader spectra (he reports seeing "the edges of things" — likely low-band IR/UV bleed); hearing range expanded; tactile sensation *reduced*, which he has discussed candidly in interviews as one of the deeper losses — he cannot reliably feel temperature, soft textures, or the subtle pressures of a handshake. He fakes the latter convincingly.
- **Metabolism:** no requirement for food, water, sleep, or oxygen. Simon continues to perform all four — eating in restaurants, sleeping in beds, breathing audibly — as social camouflage and as ritual self-anchoring. The eating in particular he describes as "the only normal thing left." He prefers steak.
- **Endocrine and reproductive function:** ambiguous and never definitively medically assessed. Sexual function is preserved (the Wanda relationship establishes this); fertility status is unknown and Simon has reportedly declined to be tested.
- **Lifespan:** indefinite. He does not age. Photographs from 1964 and from the present day are superimposable.

### Initial death event

The first transformation was unstable. Within approximately 96 hours of his turning on Zemo to save the Avengers, Simon's vital signs ceased, cellular activity arrested, and he entered the inert state that was treated as death by all parties for nearly a decade in-universe. **Cause of "death": ionic cellular saturation exceeding integrative threshold; the body could not sustain the energy load and powered down.** His remains were preserved by the Avengers in a sealed crypt at the original Mansion — a fact whose psychological significance (he was *kept*, like a relic) Simon has never fully addressed.

The dissociative interval — the years in which he was neither dead in the cellular sense nor alive in the conscious sense — is the etiological core of his subsequent PTSD presentation. He has no continuous memory of this period, but he has fragmentary impressions, primarily of cold and of being "watched from above," which he reports under direct questioning and not otherwise.

---

## III. POST-RESURRECTION ERA (~Ten years of inert preservation, then revival)

### Revival sequence

Reactivation via the Black Talon / Living Laser intervention and subsequent Avengers stabilization restored cellular ionic flow. Initial post-revival state was catatonic for approximately 48 hours, followed by a 6–9 month period of severe psychological symptomatology with somatic correlates:

- **Combat freeze responses,** documented across at least a dozen mission reports. Pulse-analogue spikes, motoric inhibition, dissociative blanking. Treated by the Avengers' in-house medical staff (Donald Blake initially, later Avengers Medical) with supportive measures only; no pharmacological intervention was attempted, partly because ionic physiology does not reliably respond to conventional psychopharmacology.
- **Sleep disturbance** despite not requiring sleep — Simon began sleeping again in this period specifically to escape consciousness, and reported nightmares of being buried alive.
- **Mild ionic instability under panic,** the first appearance of the form-destabilization that would become the defining medical feature of his later years. Initially manifested as visible "shimmer" at the periphery of his body during anxiety spikes.
- **Reconsolidation** over approximately 18–24 months, culminating in the Wrecking Crew engagement in which he forced himself through a panic response and held form under sustained blunt assault. He has described this as the closest he has come to a "cure," though it was symptomatic remission, not resolution.

### Late 1970s — early 1980s baseline

- Functionally healthy by the operational standards of the Avengers' roster.
- Ongoing low-grade depersonalization, episodic, particularly in mirrors and on awakening.
- Increased somatic vigilance — Simon began conducting private self-checks (flexing, lifting, testing density) as a daily ritual. This has continued, in some form, throughout his life.

---

## IV. THE HOLLYWOOD YEARS — INJURIES, EXPOSURES, COSMETIC INTERVENTIONS

The relocation to the West Coast and the stuntman/actor career layered an entirely new injury profile onto the ionic body. None of the injuries were medically serious — the body absorbed them — but they are catalogued because they constitute *deliberately courted* harm, which is its own diagnostic datum.

- **Pyrotechnic exposures, repeated.** Simon worked without standard protective gear on multiple productions because he didn't require it. No injury, but the visual record shows the ionic body's response to high-temperature exposure: a subtle red-shift in the skin tone for hours afterward, occasional minor flares.
- **High-fall sequences performed without rigging.** Practiced regularly. Self-reported as therapeutic — "the only time I'm sure I won't die." Note the inversion of normal stuntman psychology.
- **One incident of impalement on a set rebar accident,** ~late 1980s, no penetration; the rebar bent. Production was halted; Simon was briefly examined by an OSHA-mandated physician who found nothing diagnostically intelligible and signed off.
- **Cosmetic dental work.** Twice. Simon's teeth, like the rest of him, do not decay, but his appearance preferences changed with fashion, and he had two rounds of cosmetic restoration performed by a Beverly Hills dentist who was paid a substantial premium for discretion and for tools rated to ionic dentition.
- **Hair.** His hair grows. Slowly, but it grows. He cuts it. The fact that his hair is the only part of him that still does something organic on its own has been mentioned by him in passing, in a way that suggests it matters to him.

### Substance exposures, ongoing absence

The Hollywood milieu offered comprehensive access to recreational pharmacology across the entire late-twentieth-century menu. Simon abstained from all of it. The abstinence is total and longitudinally documented. Friends from the period describe him as the designated driver of every party he attended for fifteen years.

---

## V. THE GRIM REAPER ENGAGEMENTS — REPEATED SCYTHE TRAUMA

Across two decades of recurring violent encounters with his brother Eric, Simon sustained:

- **Multiple superficial scythe lacerations,** healed without scar; the ionic substrate reknits within minutes to hours.
- **One near-decapitation event,** in which the scythe's necro-energy channel briefly disrupted ionic cohesion at the cervical level. He reformed. The psychological residue of this engagement — being held at the edge of structural failure by his own brother — is more significant than the physical sequela, which was nil.
- **Necro-ionic interference effects,** transient. Eric's scythe was specifically tuned, in later iterations, to disrupt ionic patterns; exposure produced what Simon described as "going thin" — a few hours of reduced density, slowed reflexes, and pronounced depersonalization following each engagement.

---

## VI. SUBSEQUENT DEATHS AND RECONSTITUTIONS

### Force Works terminal event

Sacrificial engagement against Kree forces produced complete dissolution of ionic form. No body to recover. By the standards of every prior physiological framework this was death; by the standards of ionic existence it proved to be dispersion.

### Discorporated phase

Recovered as a non-corporeal ionic energy pattern persisting in proximity to Wanda Maximoff, who was — without consciously understanding she was doing so — maintaining his coherence through hex-energy expenditure. During this phase:

- No physical form sustained without external focus.
- Sensory input filtered through Wanda's perception in ways neither of them fully mapped.
- Brief manifestations of partial corporeality, increasing in stability over months.
- Eventual restoration to apparent solid form, with permanent alteration to the ionic substrate: it is now demonstrably more responsive to emotional load.

### The post-Disassembled era and progressive instability

Following the catastrophic emotional events of the mid-2000s, Simon's ionic form has exhibited:

- **Flare events:** uncontrolled luminous discharges, typically during acute affective spikes. Range from low-grade glow (an embarrassment) to full-body luminescence visible at distance (a tactical liability).
- **Dispersion episodes:** partial loss of cohesion, lasting seconds to hours, in which portions of his form become translucent or absent. He has, on documented occasion, lost a hand for the better part of an afternoon.
- **Reconstitution events:** spontaneous, often following sleep or solitude, sometimes requiring external support (proximity to other powered individuals, or to Wanda specifically, has measurable stabilizing effect).
- **Energy-form periods:** voluntary or involuntary dissolution into a coherent but non-anthropomorphic plasma state, from which restoration to human form requires concentrated effort.

These are not separate conditions. They are the same condition — a body that has become the substrate of an emotion-regulation problem. The medical and the psychological are no longer separable in Simon's case; they describe the same variable from two angles.

---

## VII. NEUROLOGICAL AND BRAIN-PATTERN HISTORY

### The engram copy

In the mid-1970s, Simon's neural patterns were recorded — non-invasively, with his knowledge but probably without informed consent in any modern sense — and the recording was used as the personality and cognitive template for the Vision. The engrams have subsequently been:

- Used as the Vision's core identity (original Vision).
- Referenced as forensic/biographical data on multiple occasions.
- Discussed, in his presence, as transferable, copyable, restorable — that is, as *not uniquely his*.

The neurological substrate is unaffected. The psychological substrate is severely affected. The fact of his own mind existing in another being, walking around married to the woman he loves, is the most singular medical-existential circumstance in this file, and it cannot be redressed by any intervention.

### Cognitive baseline

Intact across all assessments. No deficits. Processing speed slightly elevated post-transformation. Memory continuous except for the original death-interval.

---

## VIII. CURRENT MEDICAL DISPOSITION

- **Chronic, relapsing identity-coherence deficit with somatic expression** (ionic form instability), partially responsive to relational stabilization, unresponsive to pharmacology, episodically responsive to focused self-regulation.
- **PTSD, chronic, recurrent,** with traumatic origin in the initial death-interval and reactivation with each subsequent dissolution event.
- **Functional immortality** with all attendant existential burdens; no organic age-related pathology anticipated.
- **Sensory hypoaesthesia** (touch, temperature), permanent.
- **Abstinent from all substances,** lifelong post-incarceration.
- **No conventional medical care needs.** No physician of record. No insurance. No pharmacy.

### Standing recommendations for any handler with a medical-coordination remit

1. Do not attempt sedation. The substrate does not respond predictably and the attempt itself will be experienced as an assault on the one form of bodily autonomy he has left.
2. In flare or dispersion events, prioritize relational and environmental stabilization — quiet, dim light, a familiar voice, ideally Wanda's if available and clinically appropriate, otherwise Henry Pym, otherwise the Beast.
3. Do not discuss his engrams, the Vision, or the original embezzlement in clinical or operational contexts unless he raises them. Each is a known destabilizer.
4. Expect him to underreport. He has spent six decades performing a body that does not need help, and he will continue to do so until the form fails publicly.
5. Note that he eats, sleeps, and breathes for psychological reasons. Permit and encourage these rituals. They are doing more clinical work than any intervention available to us.

— *End Medical History. Cross-reference: Psychological Workup; Relational Map (Maximoff, W.; Williams, E.; Pym, H.); Incident Log (Discorporation Events).*


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS — SIMON WILLIAMS / WONDER MAN

*The body is the document. Where the file in §3 records what he believes about himself, this section records what his body confesses regardless. Every observation below is derived from longitudinal canon: the way he stands when Wanda enters a room, the way his jaw works before he says something stupid, the way ionic light bleeds from his sockets when he is losing. Because his physical substrate is no longer organic in the conventional sense, certain markers (pulse, perspiration, pupil response) are absent or transposed; the file notes those substitutions with care. The body of Simon Williams is a performance of a body — which makes every involuntary leak from it diagnostically gold.*

---

## 1. STANDING ARCHITECTURE & STATIC POSTURE

**Resting height carriage:** 6'1" frame habitually extended an additional half-inch by deliberate spinal lift — shoulders rolled back, sternum forward, chin level or fractionally elevated. This is not military posture; it is *photographic* posture, the carriage of a man who has been taught (or has taught himself) to occupy a viewfinder. It precedes the Hollywood career by years; the West Coast era only systematized what was already there.

**Weight distribution:** in repose, weight loaded ~60/40 onto the right leg, left knee soft, left foot turned out ten to fifteen degrees. This is the contrapposto of a man who expects to be looked at. He cannot stand neutrally for long; within forty seconds an unobserved Simon will drift into a presentational stance even when alone in a room (observed in solitary scenes across the Englehart and Busiek runs).

**Hand defaults:** thumbs hooked into belt or pockets, or one hand braced flat against the hip with elbow flared — wide, space-claiming postures. The opposite default — hands clasped low in front, the genital-protective "fig leaf" — appears only in two contexts: standing before Wanda when their status is undefined, and standing before an Avengers tribunal or assembled team that has reason to be displeased with him. The body knows the difference between display and judgment and configures accordingly.

**Head position under observation:** three-quarter turn preferred, never full frontal for sustained periods. He offers profiles. Under direct unblinking attention from someone he wants to impress, the head will fractionally retreat and angle, presenting the jawline. This is so deeply ingrained that he does it to mirrors.

**Head position when alone or unobserved:** drops. Chin descends three to four degrees. Shoulders un-roll. The lift is voluntary maintenance; the default substrate is mild forward collapse.

---

## 2. GAIT & LOCOMOTION

**Standard walk:** long-strided, slightly heavier heel-strike than his actual ionic mass requires — he *performs* weight, having decided early that lightness reads as flighty or feminine and weight reads as power. The stride is approximately 30–32 inches, arms swinging in moderate counter-rotation, hands loose-cupped rather than fisted.

**Walking among teammates:** he matches pace to whoever in the group has the highest social standing in that moment, settling a half-step behind their shoulder. With Wanda, dead-level; with Captain America present, the half-step behind; with civilians or the press, half-step ahead.

**Walking onto a set, into a press gaggle, or into a public Avengers appearance:** the stride lengthens by roughly two inches, the heel-strike sharpens, the arm swing increases. There is a particular shoulder-roll on the third or fourth step — a settling-into-frame motion that anyone who has watched red-carpet footage will recognize. He is unaware he does this.

**Flight posture:** arms forward, body slightly inclined head-down — the classic comic-book Superman line — when he wants to be seen flying. When traveling alone with no observers, the posture goes lazy: arms loose at sides, body near-vertical, drifting rather than driving. Two completely different aerial bodies depending on audience.

**Combat footwork:** wide base, weight low, surprisingly orthodox boxer's stance for a man who can punch through tank armor. He learned to fight as a human and never updated the schema; the ionic body executes a middleweight's mechanics at planetary force. Lead foot pivots before the cross — a tell any trained opponent (the Reaper exploits this, repeatedly) can read.

**Freeze response in combat (post-resurrection era, recurs under stress thereafter):** a specific arrest pattern — front foot lands, rear foot fails to advance, hands rise to mid-chest height and stop. The eyes go to middle distance. Duration varies: in the original phobia arc, full seconds; later in life, fractional but still observable. The Wrecking Crew breakthrough in *Avengers* #194 did not eliminate the freeze; it taught him to push through it. The micro-arrest is still there, every time, beneath the override.

**Retreat / exit walks:** when leaving a confrontation he has lost (a Wanda conversation, an Avengers admonishment), the stride shortens, the shoulders un-roll, and he produces a single backward glance at the threshold — never a full turn, just a head-swivel of perhaps thirty degrees. It is a check for whether he is being watched leave. He almost always is, and he almost always wishes he were not.

---

## 3. FACIAL ATLAS

**Resting face:** mouth fractionally upturned at the corners — a habitual half-smile that is not happiness but a social ready-state. The brow is mobile, expressive, slightly over-active; he uses it for emphasis even mid-sentence in casual conversation.

**Eyes (powered-down baseline, when depicted as human-passing):** dark brown, alert, with a tendency toward longer-than-average direct gaze when speaking — he *looks at* the person he is addressing, sometimes uncomfortably so, because he is reading them for confirmation. The gaze breaks when *he* is confirmed; he will look away the moment he sees in your face that you accept what he is saying.

**Eyes (powered-up, normal range):** uniform red luminescence, no visible iris or pupil. This is the canonical depiction. The luminescence brightens with arousal of any kind — combat, anger, sexual interest, joy at recognition. He has no biological feedback to suppress this; everyone in the room can see his affect.

**Eyes (high stress, ionic destabilization):** bleed beyond the orbit. Filaments of red-orange light visible at the lash line, the inner canthus, occasionally trailing down the malar surface like luminous tears. The Bendis/Remender-era flares are the dramatic exhibit; the micro-version of this happens routinely whenever he is genuinely overwhelmed and surrounded by people who can see it. He turns away. The turning-away is itself a tell.

**The smile inventory** — Simon has at least five distinguishable smiles and they sort by context with high reliability:

- *The press smile:* wide, teeth-prominent, asymmetric (right corner higher), held a quarter-second past natural. He learned this. It is a manufactured object.
- *The locker-room smile:* tight-lipped, brief, accompanied by a head-tilt and a single low chuckle. Deployed with male teammates after a quip lands. Genuine pleasure but routed through the bravado pipeline.
- *The Wanda smile:* slow onset, asymmetric the other way (left corner first), eyes engage before mouth, often closes back to neutral without his noticing the transition. The most honest expression in his repertoire. Observable from the West Coast run onward, intermittently through the Force Works and Busiek eras, vestigially even after she has refused him.
- *The Pym smile (or any-broken-friend smile):* small, sad, eyes soft, mouth barely moving. Reserved for moments of solidarity with a person who is suffering. He is the only Avenger who reliably wears this expression at Hank Pym during the worst of it.
- *The pre-bad-decision smile:* a flicker, gone in under a second — corners up, eyes hard. It precedes the Vision-template refusal, it precedes the Revengers' first public statement. If you saw it on a polygraph monitor you would mark the moment.

**Jaw / oral region under stress:** masseter activation — a faint pulsing along the jawline, more pronounced on the right side. He clenches when listening to criticism, particularly criticism he believes is justified. Lips compress, then release into a deliberate exhale through the nose. He does this before answering anything difficult.

**Tongue-against-teeth tell:** a brief horizontal sweep of the tongue against the front upper teeth before delivering a line he has rehearsed mentally — preceding both scripted dialogue on a set and the "spontaneous" speeches he gives to the Avengers and the press. The line is never as spontaneous as it sounds; the tongue-sweep gives him away.

**Nostril flare:** present under anger, more under shame. Shame produces a deeper, slower flare and a downward gaze. Anger flare is sharper and the eyes stay up.

**Blink rate:** baseline approximately 16–18 per minute when calm and engaged. Drops to near-zero when he is performing for cameras (deliberate suppression, learned). Spikes above 25 when he is being asked about his original conviction, his death(s), or whether he is "really" Simon. The blink-spike is the most reliable single autonomic signature in his repertoire.

---

## 4. VOICE & VOCAL HABITS

**Baseline:** baritone, well-supported, with a slight nasal resonance on long vowels — Jersey origin still detectable to a careful ear in words like *bought, talk, on*, though he has worked to neutralize it.

**Pitch under stress:** drops rather than rises. He has trained himself, consciously or otherwise, to deliver bad news and difficult statements in his lowest register. The drop is audible and over-controlled; it sounds like calm being performed rather than experienced.

**Filler words:** *"Look,"* deployed before a justification — almost a verbal tic when explaining a moral position he is uncertain of. *"I mean —"* with a slight upward inflection, used as a thinking-pause. *"The thing is —"* as the leader of any extended self-defense.

**Laughter inventory:**
- A short, single-syllable *"Ha,"* almost a punctuation mark, deployed after his own joke before anyone else has reacted. Insurance laughter.
- A genuine three- or four-pulse laugh, mouth open, head tilted back roughly fifteen degrees, with Wanda or Pym or in the rare moments when a fight is going well and he has forgotten to be afraid.
- A breathy, near-silent laugh through the nose, used when something is funny but he is supposed to be serious — most often during Avengers meetings where Clint or Hawkeye-equivalent has said something he should not encourage.

**Speech under acute stress or shame:** rate increases by perhaps 15%, sentence fragmentation increases, hand gestures expand outward as if to push the sentence into being. He talks *through* the difficulty rather than pausing inside it. The opposite of someone who collects himself before speaking — he uses speech to collect himself, often badly.

**Silence:** he does not tolerate it well. In any conversation longer than four exchanges, Simon will be the one who breaks a pause. The exception is with Wanda, where he has learned, slowly, to wait.

---

## 5. HANDS, MICRO-GESTURES, & FIDGETS

**Dominant hand:** right. Gesture register: wide, open-palmed, with the fingers slightly splayed — the gestures of an actor trained to read at distance. He does this in private conversation too. He cannot turn it off.

**Self-touch patterns:**
- *Sternum touch* — flat palm to upper chest — when accepting a compliment or being thanked. Tells the speaker "I receive this," but also reassures himself that he is solid in that moment.
- *Throat-clear with hand-to-collar* — when challenged on a position he has staked publicly. The hand reaches the collar but rarely settles, returns to his side.
- *Back-of-neck rub* — left hand, slow, when reflecting on an old failure. Most visible in any scene where the embezzlement or original death is raised.
- *Hair-smooth* — a small forward sweep of the right hand over the hairline, particularly before entering a room he expects to be looked at in. It is the closest thing he has to a pre-performance ritual.

**Fidget under boredom:** none of the usual — no pen-clicking, no foot-jiggle. He sits unnervingly still in tedious meetings, because stillness photographs better. The internal restlessness is real but is routed entirely into the eyes, which scan.

**Fidget under genuine anxiety:** the right thumb rubs against the pad of the right index finger in a slow circular motion, hand resting on thigh or chair arm. Almost invisible. Almost certainly unconscious. Present in the post-resurrection arc, present during the Vision-template debate in his own head before he refuses, present in nearly every Revengers planning scene.

**Handshake:** firm without being crushing — he has thought about this. The ionic body could pulverize bone; the handshake calibrates within civilian normal-strong range. He maintains contact for approximately one beat longer than the other party expects, and watches their eyes during the hold. Reading.

**The Wanda-hand:** when he and Wanda are co-located and on speaking terms, his right hand drifts toward her — toward the small of her back, toward her elbow, toward the space between them on a table. Often it stops short of contact, settles in the intervening air, and withdraws. He is rarely aware of doing this. Observable across the West Coast run, the Force Works era, and intermittently in every subsequent run where they share a panel.

---

## 6. GROOMING & PRESENTATION DISCIPLINE

**Hair:** dark, thick, worn at a length that requires regular maintenance. He is conscious of it. The cut updates with the decade — longer and feathered in the West Coast era, shorter and more architectural in the 2000s-onward modernized period, but always groomed. He visits a stylist at intervals shorter than most male civilians and significantly shorter than most superhumans.

**Shaving:** clean-shaven is the baseline. The ionic transformation means facial hair grows slowly if at all; he has nevertheless been observed performing the ritual of shaving — lather, blade, towel — even when functionally unnecessary. The ritual is the point. It is one of the few daily activities that confirms the body as a body.

**Skin care:** routinized. Moisturizer, sunscreen on set days (the photographic eye is sensitive to ionic luminescence under bright light, and he believes — without evidence — that surface care matters). Closet contains an unreasonable number of identical white t-shirts.

**Wardrobe (off-duty):** trends toward fitted, layered, slightly more expensive than necessary. Leather jackets recur. He buys dark colors that flatter the ionic complexion. He has *opinions* about denim.

**Wardrobe (on-duty, costume):** the original red-and-green Zemo-issue suit was loud to the point of camp; he wore it long past taste because it was his first identity object. Successive redesigns trend toward black-and-red, more functional, less iconic. He participates in the redesigns; he has opinions about silhouette. Vanity is operationalized.

**Cologne:** present in modest quantity, applied to the throat and inner wrists. Whether his ionic skin actually retains it is unclear. He applies it anyway.

**Mirror behavior:** he checks. Not constantly, but reliably — bathroom mirrors, reflective elevator panels, store windows. The check is brief and evaluative. He is monitoring whether the surface still looks like Simon Williams.

---

## 7. SLEEP, FOOD, AND THE METABOLIC ABSENCES

**Sleep:** not biologically required. He sleeps anyway, intermittently — perhaps three to five hours per night-cycle when in a stable run, sometimes none for days. The sleep is voluntary and ritualized: he undresses, gets into a bed, lies down. Whether he loses consciousness is variable; whether he dreams is genuinely unclear and a question he avoids being asked.

The sleep ritual serves the same function as the shaving ritual: it asserts that he is still a person who lives in a body in time. The absence of biological need has not eliminated the psychological need for the structure of a day.

**Insomnia equivalent:** when he cannot achieve the sleep-like state, he reads, watches old films, or — in the West Coast era and after — runs lines from scripts. He does not drink. He does not exercise (the body does not require it). The night-hours are long and he has not found a stable filler.

**Food:** not required. He eats anyway, in social contexts — meals with teammates, dates with Wanda, public appearances. He has favorite foods (Italian, specifically the heavier red-sauce end of it; a Jersey-origin preference that survives every other update). Whether his body extracts anything from the food is unclear; the act of eating with others is the function.

He has been observed declining food in private when alone. The performance is for others.

**Drink:** as noted in the Medical section, conspicuously sober. The non-drinking is over-determined: ionic metabolism may not process alcohol meaningfully; he distrusts further loss of control; the actor-milieu makes sobriety a deliberate identity marker. He orders club soda with lime in social settings and does it smoothly enough that few notice.

**Smoking:** never. Even in eras and milieus where it would have been ambient, he abstains. The lungs-as-decoration argument applies but doesn't fully explain it; he simply does not.

---

## 8. SEXUAL & INTIMATE SOMATICS

**Baseline orientation toward intimacy:** he wants it badly and approaches it cautiously. The ionic body is functionally capable; whether it is experientially equivalent to a biological body is a question he does not raise and Wanda, to her credit, has not made him answer.

**Approach behavior with Wanda specifically:** the hand-drift described above is the diagnostic. He initiates contact with surfaces of her — the back, the shoulder, the side of the face — more than with the front of her. He kisses with eyes closed and a slight forward lean from the waist, weight on the balls of the feet. After a kiss he tends to draw back and look at her face before resuming. Reading, again. Always reading.

**Post-coital behavior (West Coast era, inferred from the run's intimacy):** he talks. Almost immediately. The words are warm and the warmth is real but the speech also functions as confirmation that the encounter happened and meant what he wants it to have meant. Wanda has been observed (in the panel grammar of those issues) putting a hand on his mouth, gently, to stop the talking.

**Sexual confidence in performance vs. private:** the public persona is sexually confident to the point of swagger. The private experience is anxious — am I doing this right, am I being chosen, will she stay. The gap is large.

**Touch from teammates:** he initiates one-armed hugs, shoulder claps, hair-ruffles toward younger members. He receives touch with brief stiffening that resolves into welcome — the receiver-stiffness is the residue of a man who was not held much as a child and learned to relish but not expect contact.

**Touch from civilians (fans, autograph-seekers):** practiced welcome, mild distaste he conceals well, hand-washing afterward when possible.

---

## 9. IONIC SOMATIC SIGNATURE — THE BODY AS WEATHER

The single feature that distinguishes Simon's somatic atlas from any biological subject's: his affect is *visible as energy*. This is not metaphor. The file notes the following signatures:

- **Calm baseline:** faint warm-glow at the skin surface, perceptible to anyone within a few feet in low light. He does not notice it. Others do.
- **Mild pleasure or pride:** brightening of the ocular luminescence by perhaps 10–15%. He has been told by Beast that he "lights up" and treats this as metaphor, which it isn't.
- **Sexual arousal:** more diffuse skin-glow, particularly across chest and forearms. Reliable and embarrassing. He keeps lights low.
- **Anger:** sharp ocular brightening, narrow-band, accompanied by faint heat radiation. Civilians in proximity report warmth.
- **Shame:** the opposite — a dimming, the ionic luminescence going *down* rather than up. This is the rarest and most diagnostic signature. He cannot fake it and cannot suppress it. If you see Simon Williams dim, you have hit something true.
- **Acute panic / identity threat:** ionic flare. The dramatic version — full-body luminescence, edges of form blurring, occasionally a partial dispersion of mass into surrounding air, followed by reconstitution. The Bendis-onward depictions formalize this; the substrate has been there since the Englehart post-resurrection arc, only milder.
- **Grief / sustained sorrow:** the form does not flare but *settles* — a heavier-than-normal posture, a perceptible weight to his movements that violates the ionic body's actual physics. He produces the *appearance* of being burdened because that is how grief is supposed to look. Whether the burden is real or rehearsed is one of the hardest questions in the file.

---

## 10. STATE-DEPENDENT SUMMARY — THE BODY BY CONDITION

**At calm and unobserved:** posture slack, chin descended, eyes dim, breathing (such as it is) shallow and slow, hands still. He looks, in these moments, smaller than his actual frame. This is the closest the body comes to being un-performed.

**At calm and observed:** the lift returns. Spine, chin, eyes, the half-smile, the hand-on-hip. The transition is smooth and takes under a second. Most observers never see the un-performed version.

**Under social stress (criticism, comparison, perceived rejection):** masseter activation, blink-rate elevation, sternum-touch or back-of-neck rub, vocal rate-up, gesture-out, ionic dimming if the criticism lands true. He talks more.

**Under combat threat:** the freeze-arrest (described above), then override. Boxer's stance, lead-foot tell, ocular brightening. If the fight goes well, the genuine laugh emerges. If badly, the flare.

**Under intimacy (Wanda specifically):** the slow asymmetric smile, the hand-drift, the close-eyed kiss with forward lean, the post-coital talking. Ionic glow diffuse and warm. The most coherent his body ever looks.

**Under identity threat (questions about whether he is really Simon, about the Vision template, about the embezzlement):** blink-spike, dimming, fidget-thumb to fidget-finger, a turning-away of the head. If pressed further: ionic instability, flare, occasional partial dispersion. He has, more than once, left a room rather than allow the question to continue.

**Under shame (his own, properly attributed):** dim, nostril-flare slow and downward, eyes drop, voice drops further, hand to back of neck. He becomes physically smaller. This is the state in which he is most capable of genuine apology and most likely to deliver one.

**Under grandiose flare (Revengers-era, ideological certainty):** posture maximal, chin up beyond level, eyes bright, gestures wide, voice in the trained low register but loud. Pre-bad-decision smile flickers. The body is most performed in exactly the moments it is most wrong. The somatic atlas confirms what the psychiatric reading suspected: when Simon Williams looks most certain, trust him least.


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS

## I. The Foundational Template: The Paterson House

Every attachment Simon Williams has formed in adulthood is a recursion on a single childhood structure, and the file should name it plainly: a household organized around a father (Sanford Williams) whose love was the currency of achievement, an older brother (Eric) who collected that currency by force of temperament, and a younger son who learned, before he could articulate it, that *being* was not enough — one had to *produce* to be seen. There is no canonical scene of Sanford embracing Simon. There are repeated canonical references — across Englehart, Stern, Byrne, and the *Wonder Man* solo runs — to Simon's memory of his father's disappointment, his brother's contempt, and the quiet certainty that the Williams name would pass to Eric in spirit even if it passed to Simon on paper. The inheritance of Williams Innovations is, in this light, not a gift but a setup: he was handed the apparatus of measurement (a company, a balance sheet, a peer-comparison against Stark Industries) precisely so it could register his insufficiency in numerical form.

The attachment style that crystallizes out of this is **preoccupied-anxious with strong avoidant defenses recruited under shame** — a hybrid that looks confident at the surface (the booming voice, the costume, the screen-ready grin) and is panicked underneath. He approaches with theatrical confidence and braces, in the same gesture, for withdrawal. He scans constantly. The eye-contact pattern, traceable across decades of art direction, is consistent: Simon looks at people too long when he wants them to like him, then breaks gaze sharply when he senses he has been weighed. This is the bodily echo of the childhood pattern — approach, monitor, brace, retreat.

## II. The Bonding Cycle

Simon bonds in a predictable choreography that has not varied across sixty years of canon. The phases:

**1. Idealization-on-contact.** New relational objects are immediately overvalued. Zemo, in the prison interview, becomes a savior within minutes. The Avengers, after a single mission, become the family he had wanted. Wanda, on first sustained contact in the post-resurrection arcs, becomes the organizing principle of his interior life. The Revengers recruits become — briefly — the only people who understand. The idealization is sincere, not strategic; he genuinely experiences these figures as larger and more luminous than they are.

**2. Performative gift-giving.** Simon offers, early and conspicuously, what he believes the bonded object wants. To Zemo: betrayal of the Avengers. To the Avengers: betrayal of Zemo. To Wanda: presence, humor, the steadiness she lost with the Vision. To Hank Pym during the breakdown arc: unconditional public defense at cost to his own standing. To Hollywood: the body, the time, the willingness to do his own stunts because he literally cannot be hurt. The pattern is a child's pattern — *here is what I made for you* — refined into adult forms.

**3. Vigilant maintenance.** Once bonded, Simon does not relax. He checks. He performs continued worthiness. The micro-behavior is observable: he initiates conversation more than he receives it, he laughs first and loudest at teammates' jokes, he positions himself physically near the people whose regard organizes him (in panel composition across the West Coast Avengers run, Simon is repeatedly drawn standing one half-step closer to Wanda than the spacing requires).

**4. Catastrophic interpretation of any withdrawal.** A teammate's bad mood, a director's note, Wanda's distraction toward the Vision — read as repudiation. The reaction is not rage; it is collapse-and-perform — increased volume, increased grandiosity, increased gesture, until either the regard is restored or the bond is severed and the cycle restarts elsewhere.

**5. Sacrificial closure.** When a bond is in extremis, Simon's instinct is to die for it. He has done so literally more than once. The death is the only gift left in the inventory; it is also, in the structure of his psychology, the only act that cannot be revoked or judged inadequate by the recipient. He cannot be told the gift wasn't enough if he isn't there to hear it.

## III. Distrust

Simon's distrust runs on a tighter, more brittle circuit than his trust does. He is slow to suspect and then, once tipped, absolute. The threshold event is almost always **a perceived hierarchy of regard** — the realization that someone he loves loves another more, or rates another higher. The Vision precipitates this with respect to Wanda. Stark precipitates it, residually, with respect to the Avengers' institutional valuation (Stark is the brother-rival reincarnated as a colleague). His own brother Eric precipitates it constantly and irresolvably.

The somatic markers of Simon's distrust are visible across the canon. He goes quiet — atypically, for him — and develops a flat, slightly performative smile that the Englehart and Busiek scripts both flag in caption. He uses second-person constructions ("you'd think a man would…") to displace the accusation he cannot make directly. He withdraws physical proximity by a measurable margin (the panel composition again — when Simon distrusts you, he is drawn farther from you than the staging requires). And he *narrates* — to himself, to teammates, to the audience — building the case for the grievance in language. The Revengers founding monologue is the mature form of this private muttering rendered public. The Avengers did not become destabilizing in his eyes the morning he announced it; he had been building the brief for years.

Critically, Simon's distrust **does not generalize.** He can distrust the Avengers as an institution while loving individual Avengers. He can distrust Wanda's choices while continuing to love Wanda. The compartmentalization is not sophisticated — it is the same mechanism that lets him love Eric privately while opposing the Reaper publicly. He cannot fully condemn anyone he has bonded to, and this is the rock his entire ethical life rests on.

## IV. Betrayal

The file must distinguish two kinds of betrayal in Simon's record: **the betrayals he commits** and **the betrayals he sustains**.

**Betrayals he commits** are almost always conscience-driven reversals of a prior commitment — he turns on Zemo to save the Avengers, he turns on the Avengers to save the world (as he sees it) in the Revengers period, he refuses the Vision's restoration to protect what he believes is the more important commitment to Wanda's wellbeing and his own truth. Each is rationalized to himself as a *promotion* of loyalty from a lesser object to a greater one. He does not experience himself as a betrayer in the moment; he experiences himself as the man finally faithful to the correct thing. The shame arrives later, when the rationalization metabolizes and the residual loyalty to the betrayed party reasserts. The Vision refusal is the cleanest case: he can give the rationale at length (Vision is not the original; the brain patterns are mine and personal; Wanda deserves better) and he cannot, decades later, look the question full in the face without flinching.

**Betrayals he sustains** are processed slowly, with disproportionate self-blame. When Wanda chooses Vision over him, he reads it as his own insufficiency rather than her preference. When the Avengers do not adequately mourn his early death — or, in some interpretations, when they do not adequately welcome his return — he constructs the grievance privately for years before voicing it. When Eric repeatedly tries to kill him, Simon's response is to keep trying to save Eric. The pattern is one of **chronic forgiveness as defense against the unbearable conclusion that he was not worth the loyalty in the first place.** To accept the betrayer's malice would require accepting one's own insufficient lovability; to forgive is to preserve the hypothesis that the bond was real and the violation aberrant.

## V. Repair

Simon is, against all expectation, one of the more reparative figures in his cohort. He returns. He apologizes — sometimes too much, sometimes too publicly, but he does it. After the Revengers collapse, he reintegrates with Avengers-adjacent operations. After his various combat refusals and ideological pivots, he reappears in costume and does the work. The mechanism here is the same mechanism that creates his instability: he cannot tolerate being held in low regard, and reparative behavior is the route back to being held in good regard. The motive is mixed (genuine remorse alloyed with intolerance of disapproval) but the behavior is real.

His repair sequence is observable:
- **Withdrawal phase** — a period (days to months in-story) of literal physical absence, often Hollywood-coded, often involving the bottle he does not actually drink from and the parties he does not actually enjoy.
- **Indirect re-approach** — small public gestures, often through media (an interview, a film role, a charity appearance) that signal availability without requiring rejection-risking direct contact.
- **Mediator-assisted return** — historically Wanda, Pym, or Beast; sometimes Cap. Simon will not knock on the Avengers' door himself; he waits to be invited by someone whose invitation he can trust.
- **Disproportionate gift on re-entry** — a sacrifice, a save, a public defense of the team to outside critics — to repurchase his standing.
- **Vigilant probation** — a period of measurably modulated behavior, fewer one-liners, more deference, until he believes the bond has restabilized, at which point the baseline performance resumes.

The repair pattern fails only when the wronged party will not participate. Wanda's withdrawal from him after Disassembled is the cleanest example: she is not psychologically available to receive the repair, and Simon, without a mirror to repair *into*, destabilizes into the discorporated form. He cannot mend a bond unilaterally because the bond is the substrate of his self.

## VI. Intimacy and Sexuality

Simon's intimacy pattern, across the canon, is monogamous in intent, monocentric in object (Wanda is the only adult attachment that has stably organized his interior life), and conspicuously low-frequency in actual depicted physical or sexual content. There are women in Hollywood; they are flickered through as set-dressing. There is exactly one love. The reason is structural: Simon does not seek sex; he seeks *being-chosen*. Sex is a side-effect of being chosen, not the goal. When Wanda chooses him in the late West Coast run, the depicted intimacy is markedly tender, somewhat awed, slightly disbelieving — he behaves like a man who has won something he was sure he would not win, and he is careful with it in the way a man is careful with a thing he expects to be repossessed.

His physical comportment in intimate scenes is observably gentler than his combat physicality would predict — the ionic body that can lift a hundred tons holds her with a deliberate, careful pressure that the Englehart-era scripts flag explicitly. The carefulness is not only erotic restraint; it is the inheritance of the death-phobia. He has experienced his own bodily uncontainability. He does not entirely trust himself not to flare.

He does not, in the canon, have sustained romantic relationships outside of Wanda that read as deep attachment. The Hollywood liaisons are companionate, performative, and short. The reading is not that he is incapable of bonding to other women; the reading is that he has organized his interior life around Wanda so thoroughly that other bonds would feel, to him, like infidelity to the only narrative that makes him real.

## VII. Dependency

Simon's dependency is **mirror-dependency**, not service-dependency. He does not need others to do things for him; he needs others to *reflect him back to himself.* The distinction is load-bearing for any handler. He can survive alone in a Hollywood apartment for months; he cannot survive without an audience, real or imagined. When isolated, he constructs imagined audiences (interviews he rehearses, scripts he writes in his head, conversations with Wanda he conducts silently in his own voice). This is the same machinery that, under extremis, manifests as literal discorporation in Wanda's vicinity: without her summoning regard, he is not there.

The dependency is not equal across his bonds. The hierarchy, roughly:
- **Wanda** — primary, structural. Without her regard he destabilizes ontologically.
- **The Avengers as collective** — secondary, identity-organizing. Without them he loses the role that lets him locate himself in the moral world.
- **Pym** — peer-mirror. Pym's regard is uniquely valuable because Pym, too, has failed publicly and shamefully and returned, and Simon's bond to Pym is in part the bond of mutual fallen-and-restored.
- **The audience** — diffuse, replaceable, constant. The film audience is the maintenance dose between the bigger mirrors.
- **Eric** — negative mirror, indispensable. His brother's hatred is also a form of regard. He has not let Eric go in part because *being hated by his brother is a confirmation that he exists distinctly from his brother* — which, given the childhood structure, is its own kind of victory.

## VIII. The Repeated Relational Template

Every significant relationship in Simon Williams' life maps onto a single structural template, with role substitutions:

> **Simon, the insufficient one, attaches to a Stronger Other who confers worth, performs to maintain that worth, encounters a Rival Other who threatens the conferring relationship, and resolves the triangulation either by sacrificial gesture or by catastrophic moral pivot.**

The substitutions:
- **Sanford / Eric / Simon** — the original. Father confers, brother rivals, Simon performs and fails.
- **Zemo / Avengers / Simon** — Zemo confers (the ionic gift, the costume, the mission), Avengers become the rival object of his loyalty, Simon resolves by sacrificial pivot (turn on Zemo, apparent death).
- **Avengers / Stark / Simon** — Avengers confer membership, Stark embodies the unreachable peer-benchmark, Simon resolves through chronic underperformance-as-protest and intermittent grandiose gestures.
- **Wanda / Vision / Simon** — Wanda confers love, Vision is the rival (and, recursively, is *made of him* — the rival is literally his own template), Simon resolves catastrophically (refusal to donate brain patterns).
- **The Avengers / the world's wellbeing / Simon** (Revengers period) — the Avengers had conferred identity, the abstract "world" becomes the higher rival-object of loyalty, Simon resolves by moral pivot away from the Avengers in the name of the larger commitment. *This is structurally identical to his original turn on Zemo, with the polarity inverted.*
- **Hollywood / serious work / Simon** — the audience confers value, "serious" artistic credibility is the rival object he can never quite secure, Simon resolves through the perpetual oscillation between blockbuster bravado and reflective interview-mode self-deprecation.

The template's most disturbing feature is its **self-referentiality** in the Vision case. The Vision is Simon's own engrams in another body. The rival for Wanda's love is *himself, rebuilt by other hands and given the woman he wanted.* No psychology could survive this cleanly. Simon's response — to refuse to be the donor of restoration — is the template breaking down on its own contradiction: he could not reconcile being his own rival, so he chose to let the rival stay dead. The shame is permanent because the act was, structurally, fratricide of the only kind he could commit.

## IX. The Brother Problem (Specific Case)

Eric Williams deserves a subsection of his own because he is the only attachment in Simon's life that **predates the ionic transformation and survives every reformulation of Simon's identity afterward.** Father is dead. Wanda comes and goes. The Avengers are an institution that admits and expels. Hollywood is a marketplace. Eric is the only person who has known Simon as Simon throughout — and Eric's knowledge is the knowledge of contempt.

The Reaper / Wonder Man dynamic across the Englehart, Stern, Byrne, and later runs is not a conventional hero-villain pattern. It is a sibling enactment in costume. Eric repeatedly refuses to kill Simon at the final moment; Simon repeatedly refuses to kill Eric at the final moment; each then accuses the other of incapacity. Each death of Eric is reversed. Each reversal is, partially, Simon's doing — he cannot let his brother be gone because being-Eric's-brother is one of the few continuous facts of his interior life.

The micro-behavior in their encounters is consistent: Simon's combat fluency degrades against Eric specifically. He pulls punches he would not pull against equivalent threats. He talks more, lands less, and ends every fight visibly depleted in a way that ionic physiology cannot fully explain. The depletion is psychic. Fighting Eric requires fighting the childhood, and the childhood always wins on points.

## X. Tells, Tics, and Micro-Patterns of Bond-State

For any observer attempting to assess Simon's relational state in real time, the following micro-indicators have proven reliable across decades of canonical documentation:

- **Volume.** Simon's speaking volume rises as his anxiety about a bond rises. The booming Hollywood voice is not his natural register; it is his stressed register, normalized into a public default.
- **One-liner density.** The frequency of quips per scene tracks inversely with felt security. The West Coast bravado peak coincides with the period of maximum uncertainty about Wanda.
- **Costume self-reference.** When Simon makes a joke about his own costume, he is regulating shame about being-perceived. The more costume-jokes, the more he feels watched and judged.
- **Use of full names.** Simon calls people by full name ("Henry Pym," "Wanda Maximoff") when he is reaching for formality as a defense against intimacy he wants but cannot trust.
- **The half-step.** Physical proximity to the regard-conferring person is regulated in half-steps. He moves toward when reassured, away when uncertain, and the increments are small enough to be unconscious.
- **The flat smile.** Distinct from the broad performer-smile. The flat smile is the distrust signal — a held expression with no eye-crinkle. It appears in panels before he speaks the grievance and sometimes for whole arcs before he acts on it.
- **Ionic flicker.** Under acute relational distress, his form visibly destabilizes. This is the somatic tell that supersedes all the others. The body cannot lie about whether the bond is holding.

## XI. Summary

Simon Williams' attachment system was built by a father whose love was conditional, calibrated by a brother who refused to share standing, ratified by a peer (Stark) against whom he could only lose, weaponized by a manipulator (Zemo) who offered worth in exchange for betrayal, partially repaired by a team that took him in, deepened and wounded by a woman who loved him second, and complicated past recovery by the existence of a synthetic rival made out of his own remembered self. The relational template is recursive, the dependency is mirror-dependency, the betrayals are loyalty-promotions misread by their victims, the repairs are real but motivated, and the body itself has become the honest reporter of bond-state when the mouth will not. He is, in attachment terms, a man whose entire interior architecture depends on being seen by the right witness — and whose tragedy, often enough, is that the right witness is looking somewhere else.


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION: DEFENSES & COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS

## Subject: Williams, Simon (Wonder Man)
## Volume: Structural Defensive Architecture, Longitudinal

---

## 0. ORGANIZING THESIS

The defensive architecture of Simon Williams is unusual in the meta-human file because it must answer a question most subjects are not forced to ask: *is there a self underneath the defenses at all, or have the defenses become load-bearing structure?* The ionic transformation literalizes the metaphor — his body is energy held in a shape, and the shape is maintained, in significant part, by the same psychic operations that keep his identity coherent. When his defenses fail catastrophically (Disassembled aftermath, Revengers turn, periods of discorporation), the body fails with them. This is not metaphor; it is observable in his power-signature telemetry. The defensive map below is therefore not just a psychological inventory but a structural one.

The architecture stratifies into four layers, from most primitive to most mature, with a small constellation of compensatory behaviors that are not defenses proper but function as the scaffolding that allows the defenses to operate without total collapse.

---

## 1. THE PRIMITIVE FLOOR (psychotic-spectrum, used sparingly)

These are the operations subject employs only under extreme load — typically post-death, post-Wanda-loss, or during ionic destabilization events. They are not characterological; their appearance is a reliable index of acute decompensation and should be logged as such by any monitoring entity.

**1.1 Somatic dissociation / depersonalization.** During and immediately after each death event (Avengers #9 original, Force Works terminus, post-Busiek discorporation periods), subject describes himself in third person, refers to "this body" rather than "I," and exhibits a flattened, distant affect even while ostensibly conversing.
